Then, I applied Mixed Chicks Leave-In Conditioner (about 50 cent piece worth). Right afterwards, I evenly distributed two 50 cent pieces worth of Shea Moisturizer Smoothie. I DEFINITELY recommend people with dry, dull, hard to curl hair use this. I am amazed at how my hair looks.
